What\'s been keeping you busy?"\nExample 5: "Jaida, I\'m over the moon about us too! I\'ve never felt this way about anyone before. You\'re right, I got a bit carried away. I\'ll make sure to be more careful and respectful of others\' things. Thanks for looking out for me, and for everyone else."\nExample 7: "Thanks for askin\', Ruthie. It was a long time ago, but it\'s still pretty vivid in my mind. I was just a kid, and my family\'s house caught fire. I got trapped in my room, but my dad came in and saved me. I was scared, but he was so brave."\nExample 8: "Aww, thanks Mirna! Would you like to join me?"\nExample 9: "Kelsie, I\'d be happy to help you understand the math concepts, but I don\'t think it\'s fair to do your homework for you.
